<rating>2</rating>< review>
We came for my husband and our friend's Birthday... Our entire group wasn't here so we waited at the bar for a while. Once everyone Arrived we notified the manager and he said that he would get us seated right away! 20+ min. At the bar and no contact with us. I had to grab another hostess to get our group seated ( at a table that had been ready since we arrived an hr prior)
Food was great! Server, very sweet. However when the Salsa dancing started, we were asked to give $5 per man for lessons. I, nor my friends could find that there would be a charge for lessons. $5 isn't a lot, but it was the principle... When I asked about the "Red Ticket" that was needed to get free lessons, the manager told us it was listed on the website... I couldn't find it on what was provided via phone "Website"
Overall, fun environment, great flamenco show, and once those salsa dancers started the place came alive.... But HORRIBLE customer service by management, super rude and unapologetic.  We spent over $400 on food and drinks while there.  A little more graciousness would have been nice... Especially for a place which only rates  an average of 3 stars on Yelp! Fun place , BAD management!!!!</review>

<Rate>3</Rate><text>Sir pizza n chicken is definitely a hole in the wall. Though I pass through the area very often, I do not frequent this establishment.

After almost 6 years, I decided to go back and support small businesses! I remember it taking a while because I believed everything was made to order. I believe it was still true, because it took a while for the food to come out!

Everything was piping hot, the pizza glistened in the sun as the oils from the cheese and sausage began to puddle up on the surface. The broasted chicken looked crispy and perfectly fried. The spuds on the other hand was more of an after thought, so I‚Äôll leave it at that.

The pizza was quite delicious, I enjoyed the freshness of it, and felt that it did a good job. I just didn‚Äôt like that the man touched the pizza crust while giving us a serving spatula. I liked the texture of the chicken, and was impressed with how juicy everything was. It was delicious, oily, and hot!

My only qualms were the lack of AC, $1 charge for a cup of water (probably from the tap, and not bottled), how he handled the pizza, and the fact that everything was just so oily!

Definitely not a place to go when looking for something healthy to eat, but they do make a mean chicken!
